[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA libFuzzer run with AddressSanitizer has detected a stack-buffer-overflow in the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction `mg_json_get` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdefined in `src/mongoose/src/json.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The overflow occurs [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen the code writes one byte past the end of a local array named `nesting`. The [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcrash is triggered by the fuzz target `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` in [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`src/mongoose/test/fuzz.c`.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During fuzz testing, `mg_json_get` performs a write of size [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m at an address [0m[1;36m62[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes into a stack-allocated buffer called `nesting`, which is only [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m bytes long. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis constitutes a stack-based buffer overflow.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  Stack-buffer-overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mCWE-[0m[1;36m121[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Observations and Findings  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The sanitizer log pinpoints the invalid write at line [0m[1;36m186[0m[39m in `json.c`.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The variable `nesting` is declared at line [0m[1;36m131[0m[39m in the same file and occupies [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbytes [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m62[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in the stack frame; the write at offset [0m[1;36m62[0m[39m exceeds its bounds.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The error is reproducible under libFuzzer with [0m[1;36m100[0m[39m iterations [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`-[0m[33mruns[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The overflow is detected immediately when `mg_json_get` attempts to advance or [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrecord a nesting level beyond the buffer capacity.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code Areas for Investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Function `mg_json_get` in `src/mongoose/src/json.c`, especially around the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmanagement of the `nesting` array and its size assumptions.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Any code paths that compute or use an index into `nesting`—for example, loops [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor recursive parsing of nested JSON structures.  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. The JSON parsing logic that leads to deep or malformed nesting, to understand [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhow the write offset can exceed the declared buffer size.  [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. The fuzz harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`src/mongoose/test/fuzz.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m as an entry point, to see which [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minputs trigger the problematic code path, even though it is not the root cause.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **All Push Sites:** Review every location where `depth++` and `nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdepth++[0m[1;39m][0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
